            });

            if (country === "US") {
                loadCCPAAddon();
            }
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithOneTrustEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithOneTrustEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            script.setAttribute("data-domain-script", DATA_DOMAIN_SCRIPT);

            return script;
        }

        function loadCCPAAddon() {
            loadScript(CCPA_ADDON.url, "text/javascript", CCPA_ADDON.options);
        }

        function preloadBannerSdk() {
            const link = document.createElement("link");
            link.href = BANNER_SDK.url;
            link.rel = "preload";
            link.as = "script";

            document.head.appendChild(link);
        }

        function oneTrustLoaded() {
            return !!(window.OneTrust || window.OneTrustStub);
        }

        console.debug('OneTrust setup', countriesWithOneTrustEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !oneTrustLoaded()) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!oneTrustLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        function shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            const countriesWithKetchEnabled = {"countries":["IN","HU","SG"]};
            if (!countriesWithKetchEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithKetchEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }
            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithKetchEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }


        function loadKetchScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            if (!shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            window.semaphore = window.semaphore || [];

            window.ketch = function () {
                window.semaphore.push(arguments);
            };

            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(document.location.search);
            var property = urlParams.has("property") ? urlParams.get("property") : "website_smart_tag";

            var scriptElement = document.createElement("script");
            scriptElement.type = "text/javascript";
            scriptElement.src = "https://global.ketchcdn.com/web/v2/config/fandom/" + property + "/boot.js";
            scriptElement.defer = scriptElement.async = true;

            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(scriptElement);
        }

        function ketchLoaded() {
            return !!window.ketch;
        }

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !ketchLoaded()) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!ketchLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (async function () {
        // const AIRGAP_URL = '<script
        // data-cfasync="false"
        // src=""
        const AIRGAP_URL = 'https://transcend-cdn.com/cm/54b0c313-5d22-47e5-92fd-f979a37d1ad0/airgap.js';
        const countriesWithAirgapEnabled = [];

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {

            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadAirgapScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            const enabled = shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) || airgapScriptForced();

            if (!enabled) {
                return;
            }

            loadScript(AIRGAP_URL, "text/javascript", {
                'data-cfasync': false
            });
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithAirgapEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function airgapScriptForced() {
            return window.location.search.includes('icPreferredCMP=airgap');
        }

        function shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithAirgapEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithAirgapEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            return script;
        }

        console.debug('Airgap setup', countriesWithAirgapEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        let geo = getGeo();

        if (geo === null) {
            geo = await waitForGeo();
        }

        if (geo) {
            loadAirgapScripts(geo);
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean(false);

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	let contentWidthPreference;

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;
	}

	if ( contentWidthPreference === 'expanded' ) {
		document.documentElement.classList.add('is-content-expanded');
	}
</script>

													<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
	(function () {
		// we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
		const videoDetails = {
			mapping: {"mediaId":"sXWp3rZ0","connatixPlaylistId":"36081eca-e784-4e30-87c3-133cf673e447","impressionsPerSession":4},
			impressionsPerSession: 4,
		};
		const videoBridgeCountries = ["AE","AG","AL","AM","AR","AT","AU","AZ","BA","BB","BD","BG","BH","BN","BO","BR","BS","BY","CA","CH","CL","CN","CO","CR","CU","CY","CZ","DE","DK","DO","DZ","EC","EE","EG","ES","FI","FR","GB","GE","GF","GG","GH","GP","GR","GT","GU","GY","HK","HN","HR","HU","ID","IE","IL","IM","IN","IQ","IR","IS","IT","JE","JM","JO","JP","KE","KG","KH","KR","KW","KY","KZ","LA","LB","LK","LT","LU","LV","LY","MA","MD","ME","MK","MM","MN","MO","MQ","MT","MU","MV","MX","MY","NG","NI","NO","NP","NZ","OM","PA","PE","PH","PK","PL","PR","PS","PT","PY","QA","RE","RO","RS","RU","SA","SC","SE","SG","SI","SK","SV","TD","TH","TN","TR","TT","TW","UA","US","UY","UZ","VE","VI","VN","ZA","ZW"];
		const tier3VideoBridgeCountries = ["GB","BE","NL","DE","AU","MX","AR","FR","MD","CA","ES","IT","PE","CO","CL","NZ"];
		let hasVideoOnPage = null;

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
			const impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
			const allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

			return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
		}

		function getCountryCode() {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
			} catch {
				return null;
			}
		}

		function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
			const countryCode = getCountryCode();

			if (!countryCode) {
				return false;
			}

			// If it's a default mapping, then check the country whitelist from the default mapping.
			if (videoDetails?.mapping?.isDefaultMapping) {
				// If the wiki is classified as a tier3 wiki, then check the country whitelist from the tier3VideoBridge whitelist.
				const allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis = tier3VideoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedTier3CountryCode) {
					return allowedTier3CountryCode.toLowerCase();
				})

				return allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			} else {
				// If not a default mapping wiki (so it's a wiki mapping), then check the country whitelist from the videoBridge whitelist
				const allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
					return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
				});

				return allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			}
		}

		window.fandomIsVideoPossible = function () {
			if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
				hasVideoOnPage =
					videoDetails.mapping &&
					isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() &&
					!hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki();
			}

			return hasVideoOnPage;
		};

		window.canPlayVideo = function () {
			return window.fandomIsVideoPossible()
		};

		if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
			document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
		} else {
			document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
		}
	})();
</script>

<dl><dd><span class="dablink"><i>For other uses, see <a href="/wiki/Queen_(Disambiguation)" class="mw-disambig" title="Queen (Disambiguation)">Queen (Disambiguation)</a>.</i></span></dd></dl>
<p><b>Queen the Plague</b> is an <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates#All-Stars" title="Beasts Pirates">All-Star</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a> as one of <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a>'s three closest <a href="/wiki/Officer" title="Officer">confidants</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c925_2-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c925-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> He formerly served as the de-facto ruler of <a href="/wiki/Udon" title="Udon">Udon</a>, a region in <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> Born as <b>Scien</b>,<sup id="cite_ref-vc2_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vc2-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> he previously was also part of the rogue scientific research team <a href="/wiki/MADS" title="MADS">MADS</a> before joining Kaidou.<sup id="cite_ref-c1017_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1017-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Due to his actions and role, he is a major antagonist in the <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country_Arc" title="Wano Country Arc">Wano Country Arc</a>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance">Appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Queen is a massive, round-figured man (evidently obese but claiming otherwise)<sup id="cite_ref-c925_2-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c925-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c935_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c935-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> with light skin. At a towering 612cm tall,<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_6-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> he is a mere centimeter shorter than his fellow All-Star <a href="/wiki/King" title="King">King</a>. Similar to <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a>, Queen is built top-heavy, with thick, tapering arms yet, compared to his upper self, smallish legs.<sup id="cite_ref-c935_5-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c935-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> After being <a href="/wiki/Mori_Mori_no_Mi" title="Mori Mori no Mi">drained</a> of his fluids by <a href="/wiki/Aramaki" title="Aramaki">Ryokugyu</a>, he became much skinnier.<sup id="cite_ref-c1053_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1053-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>His head is hunched, undistinguished from his neck due to its plumpness, with a small face. His eyes are hidden by sunglasses with blue lenses and gray, oval rims, which instead of having temples are strapped on by black tapes that go around his head in such a way as to form an X both on his forehead and occiput. Queen has no visible eyebrows, a small hook nose, and his small mouth, sporting navy lipstick, always smokes a big cigar. His hair is blond: a thick, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Queue_(hairstyle)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Queue (hairstyle)">queue</a>-like braid through eight ties, with a stinger-shaped ending tuft, comes out the back of his head, which is otherwise bald. Additionally, he dons a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fu_Manchu_moustache" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Fu Manchu moustache">Fu Manchu moustache</a> whose tendrils widen as they droop to his chest. A stitched scar runs curvilinear from his right chest up to the shoulder. On Queen's upper right arm is a black (dark blue in the anime) tattoo consisting of his crew's Jolly Roger above his name in block capitals. Queen's left arm, up to the shoulder, is cybernetic in gray and golden color, composed of metallic rings, bolted plating, wiring, and even a small pressure gauge, with the corresponding hand covered in an orange glove,<sup id="cite_ref-c925_2-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c925-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c935_5-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c935-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> but was later destroyed by Sanji during the Raid on Onigashima.<sup id="cite_ref-c1034p8-9_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1034p8-9-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Queen wears large, very high-waisted overalls that uniformly reach just below the chest, are thickly, vertically striped black-and-white, and held up by suspenders connecting with 8-shaped, golden clasps on the frontal top edge; a piece of cloth striped the same is integrated into his metal arm. As for footwear, Queen has simple, brown ankle boots.<sup id="cite_ref-c935_5-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c935-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As a child, he was chubby and shaved his hair to a buzzcut. He wore dark overalls and a pair of goggles on his forehead.<sup id="cite_ref-sbs103_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs103-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During his time in <a href="/wiki/MADS" title="MADS">MADS</a> over 20 years ago, he was thin and had no facial hair. His hair was seemingly dyed and styled in a mohawk-like hairstyle. He had sunglasses and multi-part earrings. He wore a light short-sleeved shirt which he kept open, trousers with vertical stripes, a belt, and dark gloves. Over time, he put on more and more weight, grew out his mustache, started braiding his hair into a queue, and mechanized his left arm.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>20 years ago, he had a shorter, pencil-style mustache.
</p>

</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 142px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 142px; height: 142px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fd/Queen%27s_Second_MADS_Appearance.png/revision/latest?cb=20240831144910" class="image"><img alt="Queen&#39;s Second MADS Appearance" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="57" height="120" data-image-name="Queen&#39;s Second MADS Appearance.png" data-image-key="Queen%27s_Second_MADS_Appearance.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fd/Queen%27s_Second_MADS_Appearance.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/57?cb=20240831144910" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Scien's second appearance during his time in MADS.

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D3&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Living up to his position as an All-Star, Queen has a loud, bombastic, and obnoxious personality that prides himself as being a lively entertainer amongst the crew, performing his signature funky song and dance to rally his subordinates. Being extremely dramatic, he tends to treat his position as his own personal show, as seen when he told <a href="/wiki/Babanuki" title="Babanuki">Babanuki</a> to make an official ranking of the current issues at Udon. He can also be rather vain while performing, as he proudly proclaimed his fat as mere muscle and how he would be much more attractive if he was not voluntarily this large.<sup id="cite_ref-c935_5-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c935-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> At the time of being assaulted by <a href="/wiki/Ryokugyu" class="mw-redirect" title="Ryokugyu">Ryokugyu</a>, he protested the loss of his corporal volume.
</p><p>Queen is also extremely arrogant with immense pride in himself and his crew as he considered the Beasts Pirates to be the strongest and the Pleasure and Waiter members of his crew to be useless dead weight due to their lack of artificial Zoan Devil Fruit powers making them incapable of being actual use to the crew itself. He also despises people who criticize him and his actions such as his fellow All Star King due to his ego as an All Star of the Beasts Pirates, as he took twisted pride in using his viruses to hurt people including his own subordinates. Queen also considered Chopper's actions of saving infected members of the Beasts Pirates to be unnecessary, and even tried to kill Chopper out of annoyance for lecturing him with his medical ethics.
</p><p>As a part of his entertainment, Queen has a sadistic penchant for blood sports, death matches and execution games; believing that the time it takes for a battle to conclude combined with the number of fighters is what determines the level of excitement in combat.<sup id="cite_ref-c937_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c937-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> To this end, Queen is fair to some extent, allowing <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a> to fight in the Great Sumo Inferno without being restricted by the <a href="/wiki/Seastone" title="Seastone">Seastone</a> <a href="/wiki/Seastone#Restraints" title="Seastone">cuffs</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c936_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c936-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> However, his execution games are nevertheless intended to be inescapable and unwinnable. He also plays unfairly by changing rules and adding newer ones which include keeping <a href="/wiki/Eustass_Kid" title="Eustass Kid">Kid</a> and <a href="/wiki/Killer" title="Killer">Kamazo</a> submerged in water until Luffy and <a href="/wiki/Hyougoro" title="Hyougoro">Hyougoro</a> die in the ring.<sup id="cite_ref-c944_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c944-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> He also has no qualms toying with the lives of his subordinates such as the Pleasures and Waiters for his own enjoyment. 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/71/Queen_Shocked.png/revision/latest?cb=20200920225723" class="image"><img alt="Queen Shocked" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="177" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Queen Shocked.png" data-image-key="Queen_Shocked.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/71/Queen_Shocked.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20200920225723" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/71/Queen_Shocked.png/revision/latest?cb=20200920225723" class="image"><img alt="Queen Shocked" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/71/Queen_Shocked.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20200920225723" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="177" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Queen Shocked.png" data-image-key="Queen_Shocked.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/71/Queen_Shocked.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20200920225723" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Queen_Shocked.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Queen's occasional face fault.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Despite his inflated ego, Queen has the capacity to quickly lose his composure in light of a dire situation. This was seen on Onigashima, when the Nine Red Scabbards suddenly showed up on the <a href="/wiki/Onigashima#Live_Floor" title="Onigashima">Live Stage</a> to attack Kaidou, with a shocked Queen wondering where they came from.<sup id="cite_ref-c986_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c986-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> He is also shown not to be fearless as he was terrified upon seeing the change in Big Mom once she regained her memory. After Big Mom abruptly fell asleep, Queen took extreme precautions to restrain the sleeping Emperor and escort her to Onigashima as quickly as possible. However, this caused him to overlook the fact that Luffy was free of his collar and of the threat he now represented to Udon.<sup id="cite_ref-c947_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c947-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> His cowardice is evident during Kaidou's brawl with Big Mom, when Queen told his subordinates not to cower only for them to accuse him of making excuses to leave Onigashima.<sup id="cite_ref-c952_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c952-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Like <a href="/wiki/King" title="King">King</a>, Queen is extremely rude and critical of his <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">crewmates</a>, as he was quick to deride his fellow <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates#All-Stars" title="Beasts Pirates">All-Stars</a> and call them names. He and King seem to have a mutual sense of disdain for <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a>, as they are quick to gang up on him when in the same room.<sup id="cite_ref-c925_2-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c925-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> He also used derogatory language when addressing his subordinates in <a href="/wiki/Udon#Prisoner_Mine" title="Udon">Prisoner Mine</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c935_5-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c935-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>According to <a href="/wiki/Daifugo" title="Daifugo">Daifugo</a>, Queen's hobbies are building weapons and viruses.<sup id="cite_ref-c948_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c948-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As a scientist, Queen is extremely proud of his scientific talents, as he flaunts his personal cybernetic modifications, which he claims to be superior to <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk" title="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</a>'s, in battle. He also enjoys proving his scientific superiority, as he demanded that <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a> use his <a href="/wiki/Raid_Suit" title="Raid Suit">Raid Suit</a> against him to allow him to compete his own technology against <a href="/wiki/Germa_66" title="Germa 66">Germa</a>'s.
</p><p>Queen also has a fondness for beautiful women, as he was seen ogling a picture of <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Hiyori" title="Kouzuki Hiyori">Komurasaki</a>, and he appears to frequent the <a href="/wiki/Flower_Capital#Red-Light_District" title="Flower Capital">Red-Light District</a> for prostitutes. His subordinates believed that he would go berserk and take his anger out on them if he found out that Komurasaki was dead.<sup id="cite_ref-c935_5-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c935-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">

  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>

<p><br />
Queen is a glutton who is extremely fond of <a href="/wiki/Foods#Oshiruko" title="Foods">oshiruko</a>, claiming it is just as important to him as the air he breathes. He is adamant in his refusal to share with anyone.<sup id="cite_ref-c937_15-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c937-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> When Queen does not get his daily fill of oshiruko, he becomes easily irritable and even murderous.<sup id="cite_ref-c944_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c944-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> Queen's love for oshiruko is so immense, that he is willing to fight the <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Emperor</a> Big Mom to prevent her from stealing his oshiruko.<sup id="cite_ref-c945_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c945-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Queen has interjected the word "Excite"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">エキサイト</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Ekisaito</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> into his sentences. The Japanese word for his epithet, "Plague", is "Ekisai"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">疫災</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>. The Viz translation retains the pun, with Queen saying phrases like "I'm plagued with excitement!".<sup id="cite_ref-c935_5-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c935-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c937_15-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c937-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Hyo_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hyo-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Like many other characters, Queen has his <a href="/wiki/Laughter_Style" title="Laughter Style">own distinct laugh</a>, "Muhahaha"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">ムハハハ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Muhahaha</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-c936_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c936-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D4&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Crew">Crew</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D5&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>While Queen acts extremely obnoxious toward his <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">crewmates</a>, he is popularly received amongst the lower-ranking members, given his music-performing nature and penchant for execution games.<sup id="cite_ref-c936_16-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c936-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> In spite of that, Queen had faith that his subordinates could defeat <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a> in a rigged sumo tournament despite the fact that Luffy had a higher <a href="/wiki/Bounties" title="Bounties">bounty</a> than Queen himself.<sup id="cite_ref-c936_16-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c936-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> Also, his crew has a sense of fear whenever Queen becomes angry, especially when he is denied <a href="/wiki/Foods#Oshiruko" title="Foods">oshiruko</a>, his favorite food.<sup id="cite_ref-c944_17-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c944-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">You Pleasures!! You already gambled on a chance to gain powers, and failed!! You're dead weight that does nothing but laugh!!! You Waiters!! There's no more shipments of SMILE fruits coming to us!!! You've lost your chance to gain powers!! You'll be waiting forever!! So if there's any way you layabouts will ever be useful to this almighty crew...it's by becoming oni in your last moments, and letting your deaths serve a glorious purpose!!!</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:&#39;Arial&#39;,sans-serif;">—&#160;Queen belittling the Pleasures and Waiters.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br />
Nevertheless, Queen holds the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates#Pleasures" title="Beasts Pirates">Pleasures</a> and <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates#Waiters" title="Beasts Pirates">Waiters</a> in little regard, involving them in a sadistic tagging game of <a href="/wiki/Ice_Oni" title="Ice Oni">Ice Oni</a> seemingly for his own amusement. Because those grunts are unable to gain <a href="/wiki/SMILE" title="SMILE">SMILE</a> abilities anymore, Queen developed the Ice Oni virus specifically to make them stronger foot soldiers for the Beasts Pirates at the cost of their own lives, admitting that he did not care whether those below the rank Gifters died or not since they were expendable and easy to replace. Feeling hurt and betrayed by this display of callousness from their superior, some of the Pleasures and Waiters decided to rebel against Queen and fight for the <a href="/wiki/Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai_Alliance" title="Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance">Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance</a>. Furthermore, he had no reservations in attacking Gifters who had been tamed by <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Tama" title="Kurozumi Tama">Tama</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Kibi_Kibi_no_Mi#Techniques" title="Kibi Kibi no Mi">Kibi Dangos</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c1022_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1022-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Queen dislikes the company of the <a href="/wiki/Numbers" title="Numbers">Numbers</a>, citing that they have drinking problems.<sup id="cite_ref-c954_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c954-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kaidou">Kaidou</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As one of <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a>'s three closest associates, Kaidou has a great deal of trust in Queen and his abilities.<sup id="cite_ref-c925_2-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c925-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> Both Kaidou and Queen have a sense of cordial respect with each other, as Queen addresses Kaidou by his name, rather than by title, such as "Sir" or "Boss".<sup id="cite_ref-c941_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c941-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> In addition, Queen's loyalty to his general is also unquestioned, as he attacked Big Mom for invading Wano.<sup id="cite_ref-c947_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c947-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Kaidou, though seeing Queen as one of his three confidants, did not hesitate in giving the lower ranking Tobiroppo a chance to challenge any All-Star of their choice to take their position, as the crew's hierarchy is determined by an individual's power.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> Kaidou also took joy to Queen's dismay when he told him of Komurasaki's "death", much to the latter's overwhelming sadness.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="King">King</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Queen has a rivalry with his fellow <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates#All-Stars" title="Beasts Pirates">All-Star</a>, <a href="/wiki/King" title="King">King</a>, as they both didn't hesitate to insult one another in front of their subordinates. However, they both share a mutual disdain toward their other fellow All-Star, <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c925_2-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c925-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> After escorting Big Mom to Onigashima, Queen furiously blamed King for Big Mom's presence. Queen shown hostility towards King and tell to stop attack randomly after being hit at the rear, only for King to mock Queen as he wish he would slice off his neck.
</p><p>In spite of this mutual animosity, Queen knows how to work together with King when the situation demands it. Furthermore, Queen is shown to have more confidence in his fellow All-Star's abilities than he ordinarily admits, as shown when he gloated to Sanji that King's lunarian heritage would allow him to make quick work out of Zoro.<sup id="cite_ref-c1033_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1033-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Jack">Jack</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Despite both being All-Stars, Queen has an extreme amount of ridicule for Jack, as he joined King in ganging up on and insulting him when in the same room. Jack was silent at this verbal abuse and only replied in a respectful tone, despite his ruthless personality.<sup id="cite_ref-c925_2-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c925-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Scratchmen_Apoo">Scratchmen Apoo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Given their shared music-loving personalities, Queen shares a close relationship with <a href="/wiki/Scratchmen_Apoo" title="Scratchmen Apoo">Scratchmen Apoo</a>, to whom he refers as "brother"<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> and shown when the two perform together at the Golden Kagura.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> Their close friendship did not stop Queen from putting Apoo in a sadistic game with all the others in a room infected with Ice Oni. He did, however, leave with him the only known antidote, albeit putting him in an even more dangerous situation. After Apoo was defeated by Zoro and the antidote was taken, Queen was disappointed and decided to infect Apoo with the virus, but Zoro destroyed the gun.<sup id="cite_ref-c997p11_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c997p11-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Straw_Hat_Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Monkey_D._Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;"><b>Queen</b>: Who do you think you're ordering around? Don't be so full of yourselves, boys. Who said you could feel hope? What makes you think you're getting out of this alive? You think you can beat us? All of you are going to die!! One by one!!!<br /><b>Luffy</b>: Shut up! The only one who decides when and where I'll die...is me!!</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:&#39;Arial&#39;,sans-serif;">—&#160;Queen and Luffy arguing.<sup id="cite_ref-c944_17-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c944-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br />
Queen has genuine respect for <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a> due to his strength and reputation as a member of the <a href="/wiki/Worst_Generation" title="Worst Generation">Worst Generation</a>, repeatedly trying to convince the Straw Hat to join the Beasts Pirates, and stating that he would personally ask his captain to pardon him for his crimes if he did, in spite of Luffy's openly rebellious attitude towards Kaidou and his crew.<sup id="cite_ref-c935_5-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c935-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> Queen was impressed that Luffy was able to use <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c936_16-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c936-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Regardless, Queen still looks down on Luffy to an extent and made sure to reiterate to the Straw Hat captain that, as long as he was his prisoner, his situation was hopeless. The All-Star also noticed that Luffy cared for <a href="/wiki/Eustass_Kid" title="Eustass Kid">Eustass Kid</a>'s well-being as a fellow rival of the <a href="/wiki/Worst_Generation" title="Worst Generation">Worst Generation</a>, taking advantage of this to motivate Luffy into losing his Sumo Inferno game by continuously torturing Kid after the latter got recaptured into Udon.
</p><p>Luffy has his own personal nickname for Queen: "Balloon".
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Tony_Tony_Chopper">Tony Tony Chopper</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Queen seemingly has a very low opinion on Chopper, viewing the reindeer as nothing more than a lowly ship's doctor and questioning his ability to counter his viral weapons. In addition, as a pirate used to treacherous practices, Queen thought Chopper was lying to the victims of the Ice Oni disease about developing a possible cure to save them, having expected the Straw Hat to have fled away despite his promises. When Chopper managed to prove him wrong and did in fact cure all victims, Queen became angry and tried to shoot the reindeer dead.
</p><p>Chopper, who is a follower of medical ethics, opposes everything Queen stands for regarding the weaponization of viruses, as the reindeer doctor believes those cannot be properly controlled by humans. As is the case with many other characters, Chopper is referred to as a tanuki by Queen. Chopper, predictably angry about this, clarified to Queen that he was in fact, a reindeer, while slapping the All-Star in the face when given the opportunity.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Unfortunately for Chopper, Queen turned out to be too much for him to handle, as the All-Star admitted he was merely playing around with the reindeer before attempting to finish him off, having decided to humor Chopper for his insolent behavior beforehand. Fortunately, though, Chopper was able to hold off Queen long enough for Sanji to arrive and take over the fight.<sup id="cite_ref-c1015p4_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1015p4-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Sanji">Sanji</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Queen is aware of <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a>'s lineage to his old lab partner, Vinsmoke Judge, constantly referring to him as "Judge's son", which irritated Sanji due to his hatred for his blood-father. He also assumed that Sanji's <a href="/wiki/Black_Leg_Style/Diable_Jambe" title="Black Leg Style/Diable Jambe">flaming kick</a> was a result of Judge's <a href="/wiki/Modified_Humans" title="Modified Humans">modifications</a> to all his children.
</p><p>He completely ignored Sanji's refusals about using the <a href="/wiki/Raid_Suit" title="Raid Suit">Raid Suit</a>, as Queen was more thrilled about seeing the Germa science in reality than having to deal with Sanji's hatred for his family. When Sanji makes the choice to destroy the Raid Suit, Queen was disappointed that he would never be able to see Sanji transform into it, as he wanted to test it against the abilities of the Vinsmoke brothers that he duplicated to prove he was a superior scientist to Judge, much to Sanji's ire who doesn't care about this rivalry.
</p><p>When Sanji later found out that Queen was the one who was actually responsible for injuring the geisha <a href="/wiki/Some" title="Some">Some</a> instead of him, for making him doubt himself, an enraged Sanji unleashed a new ability called <a href="/wiki/Black_Leg_Style/Ifrit_Jambe" title="Black Leg Style/Ifrit Jambe">Ifrit Jambe</a> to assault Queen with a chain of attacks, with Sanji ordering Queen to never say the names of his father and brothers in his presence, which resulted in Queen's defeat.<sup id="cite_ref-c1035_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1035-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Hyougoro">Hyougoro</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Queen is familiar with <a href="/wiki/Hyougoro" title="Hyougoro">Hyougoro</a> as the legendary yakuza boss of the <a href="/wiki/Flower_Capital" title="Flower Capital">Flower Capital</a>. After they first met, Queen mocked Hyougoro for his miserable plight and also sentenced him to the Great Sumo Inferno as a death sentence.<sup id="cite_ref-Hyo_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hyo-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> Nevertheless, he was impressed by the latter's strength.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later, during the Onigashima raid, Queen witnessed Hyougoro regaining the strength of his prime thanks to the <a href="/wiki/Ice_Oni" title="Ice Oni">Ice Oni</a> disease and wiping out a large number of Kaidou's forces at the Live Stage. This led the All-Star to acknowledge the old yakuza boss as a significant threat, enough to target him.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="X_Drake">X Drake</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Because of his role as a <a href="/wiki/SWORD" title="SWORD">traitor</a> who freed <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Trafalgar Law</a> while the latter was captive under the Beasts Pirates, Queen obviously despises Drake and intended to kill him during the Golden Kagura. Queen and <a href="/wiki/Who%27s-Who" title="Who&#39;s-Who">Who's-Who</a> both orchestrated an ambush in order to catch Drake off-guard and proceeded to interrogate him about his true allegiance. Later on, when Drake escaped into the Live Stage, Queen stated that there was no escape for the former Tobiroppo before starting the <a href="/wiki/Ice_Oni" title="Ice Oni">Ice Oni</a> outbreak.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Charlotte_Linlin">Charlotte Linlin</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As Big Mom is his general's rival, Queen knows very well who she is and seems to be afraid of her, as he was very scared when he saw her appear in <a href="/wiki/Prisoner_Mine" title="Prisoner Mine">Prisoner Mine</a>. However, this did not stop Queen from wanting to confront the Emperor upon hearing that she wanted to eat his favorite food, although this only caused Big Mom to hit him.<sup id="cite_ref-c945_23-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c945-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Despite being overpowered, Queen still wanted to prevent the Emperor from causing further damage to Udon, devising a strategy to do so. But when that didn't work either, causing even Big Mom to regain her memory and recognize him, the All-Star finally succumbed to fear. However, Big Mom fell asleep, so Queen proceeded to take her to Onigashima, although with many precautions to contain her, since he knew that if the Emperor woke up he would be in trouble.<sup id="cite_ref-c947_19-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c947-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite his fear of her, Queen still showed his disrespect towards Big Mom while the latter was handcuffed, calling her an "old hag" and refusing to release her until Kaidou appeared.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Others">Others</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Komurasaki">Komurasaki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Queen is immensely infatuated with <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Hiyori" title="Kouzuki Hiyori">Komurasaki</a>, believing that her beauty is wasted on the Shogun <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Orochi" title="Kurozumi Orochi">Orochi</a> and even carrying around her picture to ogle at in his free time. Queen's adoration for Komurasaki is so great that his subordinates are terrified of reporting her death to Queen in fear that he will kill them in a fit of rage.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> When Queen found out about her "death", he started crying and begging for it to be a lie.<sup id="cite_ref-c941_28-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c941-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Some">Some</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After Komurasaki's death, Queen moved on to <a href="/wiki/Some" title="Some">Some</a>, a young geisha from the <a href="/wiki/Flower_Capital" title="Flower Capital">Flower Capital</a> to which he considered his new number one. However, the geisha held no interest in Queen at all and frequently made up excuses to avoid servicing him. This angered Queen, who later discovered Some's truth and attacked her when he had the chance. He then attempted to do it again upon seeing the geisha still healthy, only for Sanji to defeat him in the process.<sup id="cite_ref-c1034_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1034-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="MADS">MADS</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Vinsmoke_Judge">Vinsmoke Judge</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>In the past, Queen and <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Judge" title="Vinsmoke Judge">Vinsmoke Judge</a> were colleagues at <a href="/wiki/MADS" title="MADS">MADS</a>. But despite having the same interest in creating weapons of destruction, the two also often fought over who was the second best in the group.
</p><p>Despite many years after the dissolution, Queen still appeared to have a rivalry with Judge, as he decided to copy the skills of the latter's children, knowing that this was the pinnacle of his former colleague's scientific work. Likewise, he believed that if he defeated Sanji with the Raid Suit, he would prove that he was a better scientist than Judge.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Similarly, Queen seemed to have a certain disdain for his former colleague <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk" title="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</a>, as the latter was dedicated to inventing products that promoted peace.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Even long after the disbandment, he still held Vegapunk in low regard, believing that his former colleague's science was inferior to his own cybernetics.<sup id="cite_ref-c1023p7_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1023p7-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>As an All-Star of the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a>, Queen has great authority over his crew just below his <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Governor-General</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c925_2-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c925-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> He formerly had the highest authority over <a href="/wiki/Udon" title="Udon">Udon</a>, a region in <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a>, and oversaw proceedings at the <a href="/wiki/Prisoner_Mine" title="Prisoner Mine">Prisoner Mine</a>, where all the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates#Shinuchi" title="Beasts Pirates">Shinuchi</a> who maintained the facility reported directly to him.<sup id="cite_ref-c935_5-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c935-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In combat, Queen proves to be extremely formidable, and his <a href="/wiki/Bounties" title="Bounties">bounty</a> of <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>1,320,000,000 demonstrates how dangerous the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a> considers him, also being the third highest bounty of the crew, only below <a href="/wiki/King" title="King">King</a> and Kaidou himself.<sup id="cite_ref-bounty_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bounty-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> He has also been a member of the crew for at least twenty years, making him a true veteran.<sup id="cite_ref-c970_43-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c970-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During the battle on <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a>, Queen exhibits extraordinary fighting skills, as he (alongside <a href="/wiki/King" title="King">King</a>), was able to battle <a href="/wiki/Marco" title="Marco">Marco the Phoenix</a>, the former right hand of the Emperor <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a>, until the latter's exhaustion, and emerged from the fight with superficial injuries, before engaging a large group of enemies.<sup id="cite_ref-c1006p17-18_44-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1006p17-18-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c1022_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1022-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> As a further testament to his power, Chopper, in his strongest form, the <a href="/wiki/Hito_Hito_no_Mi#Monster_Point" title="Hito Hito no Mi">Monster Point</a>, was utterly helpless before Queen, being quickly overwhelmed when the All-Star decided to take the fight seriously, and being unable to inflict any substantial damage on him during a time span of at least twenty minutes.<sup id="cite_ref-c1015p4_35-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1015p4-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_Abilities">Physical Abilities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Queen has demonstrated incredible fighting skills by combining his vast physical strength with his cybernetics, being capable of easily blocking one of <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a>'s punches with his hand and throwing the pirate to the ground with his mechanical arm.<sup id="cite_ref-c944_17-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c944-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> He could fight and overwhelm <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a>, an extremely powerful martial arts master, slamming him through multiple reinforced stone walls with a single hand.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> However, Queen's fighting prowess has limits, as he was completely unable to track Sanji's newly acquired high speed movement after his genetic enhancements were fully awakened, which he initially mistook for invisibility, and was quickly defeated by his barrage of <a href="/wiki/Black_Leg_Style/Ifrit_Jambe" title="Black Leg Style/Ifrit Jambe">Ifrit Jambe</a>-enhanced techniques.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> He is also shown to have enough durance to somehow survive the fall when Sanji kicked him out of Onigashima while it was being lifted into the sky.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Engineering_Expertise">Engineering Expertise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Queen is an extremely talented <a href="/wiki/Scientist" title="Scientist">scientist</a>, inventor, and mechanic who specializes in the creation of biological weaponry, perfecting these skills to the point of creating numerous man-made viruses, and designing and modifying himself with advanced enough cybernetics to replicate the <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Family" title="Vinsmoke Family">Vinsmoke Family</a>'s abilities as <a href="/wiki/Modified_Humans" title="Modified Humans">Modified Humans</a>, even developing modifications and weaponry for his Zoan form as well. Queen is also skilled at developing brutal torture machines and uses them as a method to break the spirits of the Beasts Pirates' enemies and get them to reveal information, an ability of which he is very proud of.
</p><p>Queen is notable for having been formerly part of <a href="/wiki/MADS" title="MADS">MADS</a>, a rogue research team involved in several scientific discoveries and development of weapons.<sup id="cite_ref-c1017_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1017-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Cybernetic_Enhancements">Cybernetic Enhancements</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/34/Queen_Neck_Extension.png/revision/latest?cb=20230113130727" class="image"><img alt="Queen Neck Extension" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="132" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Queen Neck Extension.png" data-image-key="Queen_Neck_Extension.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/34/Queen_Neck_Extension.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230113130727" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/34/Queen_Neck_Extension.png/revision/latest?cb=20230113130727" class="image"><img alt="Queen Neck Extension" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/34/Queen_Neck_Extension.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230113130727" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="132" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Queen Neck Extension.png" data-image-key="Queen_Neck_Extension.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/34/Queen_Neck_Extension.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230113130727" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Queen_Neck_Extension.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Queen's mechanical extensions.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Queen employs several <a href="/wiki/Cyborgs" title="Cyborgs">cybernetic augmentations</a> of his body that greatly assist him in battle. He claims to be a cyborg<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja"><ruby lang="ja"><rb>絡繰人間</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>サイボーグ</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby></span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">saibōgu</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "mechanical human")</span> so technologically advanced that even <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk" title="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</a>, the world's greatest scientific genius and Queen's ex-colleague, would not be able to replicate him.<sup id="cite_ref-c1023p7_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1023p7-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> Queen has multiple high-tech weapons and mechanisms installed within his body, which he usually activates while employing his Zoan abilities. Among his enhancements are laser beams, metal grappling claws, rocket launchers and extendable mechanized limbs. 
</p><p>In his full brachiosaurus form, he has a double-barreled Gatling gun, artificial fangs and a laser beam cannon equipped at the end of his brachiosaurus tail and hair braid, as well as inside of his mouth, with the latter in particular being an extremely advanced form of technology that has only been replicated by master engineers like <a href="/wiki/Franky" title="Franky">Franky</a> and Vegapunk, a testament to Queen's own genius. Moreover, his neck area is modified with an in-built mechanical cable that allows him to extend his already long brachiosaurus neck beyond its normal range. He also has retractable needles in his teeth and voice activated rocket launchers in his sides.
</p><p>Queen's hybrid form displays a different set of modifications, such as clawed tentacle appendages located on his tail and braided hair, which is also capable of firing lasers. His prosthetic left arm also changes shape, sporting a claw similar to the aforementioned appendages. His left arm was later destroyed by Sanji during the Raid on Onigashima.<sup id="cite_ref-c1034p8-9_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1034p8-9-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Notably, Queen has done significant research on <a href="/wiki/Germa_66" title="Germa 66">Germa 66</a>'s technology, with the intent of surpassing it through his own cybernetic replications. As such, Queen has access to most of the special powers held by the Vinsmoke siblings in their <a href="/wiki/Raid_Suit" title="Raid Suit">Raid Suits</a>, such as <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Ichiji" title="Vinsmoke Ichiji">Ichiji</a>'s optic beams, <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Niji" title="Vinsmoke Niji">Niji</a>'s lighting shocks, <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a>'s invisibility, and <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Yonji" title="Vinsmoke Yonji">Yonji</a>'s extendable metal arm.<sup id="cite_ref-Germa_powers_48-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Germa_powers-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Techniques">Techniques</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D28&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f0/Black_Coffee.png/revision/latest?cb=20221002020825" class="image"><img alt="Black Coffee" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Black Coffee.png" data-image-key="Black_Coffee.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f0/Black_Coffee.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20221002020825" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f0/Black_Coffee.png/revision/latest?cb=20221002020825" class="image"><img alt="Black Coffee" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f0/Black_Coffee.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20221002020825" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Black Coffee.png" data-image-key="Black_Coffee.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f0/Black_Coffee.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20221002020825" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Black_Coffee.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Queen using Black Coffee.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
