<ul><li><b>Black Coffee</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">ブラック<ruby lang="ja"><rb>光火</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>コーヒー</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby></span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Burakku Kōhī</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "Black Light Flame")</span>: In his Full Beast Form, Queen fires a <a href="/wiki/Laser" title="Laser">laser</a> beam from his mouth or tail, while in his human-beast form he can fire it (individually or simultaneously) from either his mouth, mechanical arm, hair, or tail.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> The beam works similarly to the ones used by the <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifista</a> and <a href="/wiki/Franky" title="Franky">Franky</a>'s "Radical Beam", generating an explosion after hitting a surface. The beam is depicted as purple and black in the <a href="/wiki/PAINT" title="PAINT">24th opening</a> of the anime. Queen first attempted to use this move against <a href="/wiki/Hyougoro" title="Hyougoro">Hyougoro</a>, but he was interrupted by <a href="/wiki/Marco" title="Marco">Marco</a> before he could fire it, causing Queen to target the former commander with this move instead.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> However, the technique was not named until Queen used it against <a href="/wiki/Tony_Tony_Chopper" title="Tony Tony Chopper">Chopper</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> This technique's name is a pun on the fact that the kanji characters for "Light Flame" (光火) can be read as <i>kō hi</i>, which resembles the Japanese pronunciation of "coffee"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">コーヒー</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">kōhī</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>. The pronunciation of "black" (<i>burakku</i>) is also similar to the "brachio" (<i>burakio</i>) prefix that is consistent with Queen's brachiosaur theme. In the VIZ manga and Funimation adaptations, this is called <b>Black Coffee Beam</b>, which is possibly a pun on "coffee bean".</li></ul>
<ul><li><b>Bridal Grapper</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">ブライダル<ruby lang="ja"><rb>熱拳</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>グラッパー</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby></span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Buraidaru Gurappā</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "Bridal Heat Fist")</span>: While in Human-Beast Form, Queen heats up his mechanical hair claw and attempts to grab a target while burning them with it. This move was first attempted on <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a>, but <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a> intervened and countered the move with his own <a href="/wiki/Black_Leg_Style/Diable_Jambe" title="Black Leg Style/Diable Jambe">Diable Jambe</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> The pronunciation of "bridal" (<i>buraidaru</i>) is similar to the "brachio" (<i>burakio</i>) prefix that is consistent with Queen's brachiosaur theme. In the VIZ manga and Funimation adaptations, this is called <b>Bridal Grabber</b>.</li></ul>
<ul><li><b>Bry Pan</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja"><ruby lang="ja"><rb>風来拳</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>ブライパン</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby></span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Burai Pan</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "Erratic Fist")</span>: While in Human-Beast Form, Queen rapidly punches with his hair claw, tail claw, and left arm claw. This was first used against Sanji.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> The name of the technique is a pun on "fry pan", with the initial syllable altered to mimic the pronunciation of "brachio" (<i>burakio</i>). In addition, the kanji characters for "erratic" (風来) would normally be read as <i>fūrai</i>, resembling the Japanese pronunciation of "fry"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">フライ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">furai</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>. In the VIZ manga and Funimation adaptations, this is called <b>Flying Pan</b>.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f7/Brachio_Launcher.png/revision/latest?cb=20230226053837" class="image"><img alt="Brachio Launcher" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Brachio Launcher.png" data-image-key="Brachio_Launcher.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f7/Brachio_Launcher.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230226053837" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f7/Brachio_Launcher.png/revision/latest?cb=20230226053837" class="image"><img alt="Brachio Launcher" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f7/Brachio_Launcher.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230226053837" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Brachio Launcher.png" data-image-key="Brachio_Launcher.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f7/Brachio_Launcher.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230226053837" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Brachio_Launcher.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Queen using Brachio Launcher.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b>Brachio Launcher</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">ブラキオランチャー</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Burakio Ranchā</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>: While in Beast Form, Queen activates rocket launchers equipped to his torso via a voice command. This was first used against Sanji, though Queen accidentally also hit himself by mentioning the "Brachio Launchers", which activated the voice recognition.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<ul><li><b>Sparking Queen</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja"><ruby lang="ja"><rb>火花</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>スパーキング</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby><ruby lang="ja"><rb>QUEEN</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>クイーン</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby></span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Supākingu Kuīn</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "Spark Queen")</span>: Queen's variant of Germa 66's <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Ichiji#Sparking_Red" title="Vinsmoke Ichiji">Sparking Red</a>, Queen fires beams from his eyes.<sup id="cite_ref-Germa_powers_48-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Germa_powers-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<ul><li><b>Henry Queen</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja"><ruby lang="ja"><rb>起電</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>ヘンリー</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby><ruby lang="ja"><rb>QUEEN</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>クイーン</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby></span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Henrī Kuīn</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "Electromotive Queen")</span>: Queen's variant of Germa 66's <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Niji#Dengeki_Blue" title="Vinsmoke Niji">Dengeki Blue</a>, Queen electrifies his body and then extends his mechanized neck in order to bite and electrocute his enemy.<sup id="cite_ref-Germa_powers_48-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Germa_powers-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<ul><li><b>Winch Queen</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja"><ruby lang="ja"><rb>巻力</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>ウインチ</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby><ruby lang="ja"><rb>QUEEN</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>クイーン</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby></span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Uinchi Kuīn</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "Winding Power Queen")</span>: Queen's variant of Germa 66's <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Yonji#Winch_Green" title="Vinsmoke Yonji">Winch Green</a>, Queen extends his mechanical left arm, grabs his opponent, and swings them around, slamming them into various walls.<sup id="cite_ref-Germa_powers_48-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Germa_powers-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Medical_Expertise">Medical Expertise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D29&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/84/Mummy_%28Virus%29_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20201025043901" class="image"><img alt="Mummy (Virus) Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Mummy (Virus) Infobox.png" data-image-key="Mummy_%28Virus%29_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/84/Mummy_%28Virus%29_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20201025043901" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/84/Mummy_%28Virus%29_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20201025043901" class="image"><img alt="Mummy (Virus) Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/84/Mummy_%28Virus%29_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20201025043901" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Mummy (Virus) Infobox.png" data-image-key="Mummy_%28Virus%29_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/84/Mummy_%28Virus%29_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20201025043901" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mummy_(Virus)_Infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A crowd of prisoners afflicted with Queen's virus "Mummy".</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Like the other All-Stars, he is hailed as a "calamity" for his destructiveness, having earned the moniker of "The Plague" due to his use of extremely potent manufactured viruses.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> In fact, had it not been for the efforts of <a href="/wiki/Tony_Tony_Chopper" title="Tony Tony Chopper">Tony Tony Chopper</a>, the doctor of the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a>, the thousands of warriors fighting on the Live Floor of the <a href="/wiki/Skull_Dome" title="Skull Dome">Skull Dome</a> would have all been wiped out after being infected by just one of his artificial viruses.<sup id="cite_ref-c1007_57-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1007-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Befitting his epithet of "The Plague", Queen is a genius virologist. He has invented abnormal and deadly viruses and weaponized them through ammunition known as <a href="/wiki/Excite_Bullets" title="Excite Bullets">Excite Bullets</a>, which instantly spread the disease upon striking their victims. Two of Queen's viruses have been seen so far, and both of them are able to easily spread through physical contact, meaning Queen and anyone with Excite Bullets can quickly infect an entire closed-off group of enemies with only a few hits.<sup id="cite_ref-c949_58-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c949-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c993_59-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c993-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> He has shown sufficient medical expertise to develop an antidote for one of his deadliest viruses as a safety measure.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Created_Viruses">Created Viruses</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D30&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Mummy_(Virus)" title="Mummy (Virus)">Mummy</a> causes a high fever and constant bleeding. Not long after, its victims become shriveled and dehydrated and suffer everlasting pain.<sup id="cite_ref-c949_58-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c949-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ice_Oni" title="Ice Oni">Ice Oni</a> covers its victims' skin in ice, which alters some parts of their bodies to make them look like <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oni" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Oni">Oni</a>. It also enhances their physical abilities. Victims are left freezing and seem to turn savage.<sup id="cite_ref-c993_59-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c993-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> The frost combined with the strength boost causes its victims to die after roughly one hour.</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Devil_Fruit">Devil Fruit</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D31&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Ryu_Ryu_no_Mi,_Model:_Brachiosaurus" title="Ryu Ryu no Mi, Model: Brachiosaurus">Ryu Ryu no Mi, Model: Brachiosaurus</a></i></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/40/Ryu_Ryu_no_Mi%2C_Model_Brachiosaurus_Beast_Form.png/revision/latest?cb=20221106024038" class="image"><img alt="Ryu Ryu no Mi, Model Brachiosaurus Beast Form" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ryu Ryu no Mi, Model Brachiosaurus Beast Form.png" data-image-key="Ryu_Ryu_no_Mi%2C_Model_Brachiosaurus_Beast_Form.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/40/Ryu_Ryu_no_Mi%2C_Model_Brachiosaurus_Beast_Form.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221106024038" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/40/Ryu_Ryu_no_Mi%2C_Model_Brachiosaurus_Beast_Form.png/revision/latest?cb=20221106024038" class="image"><img alt="Ryu Ryu no Mi, Model Brachiosaurus Beast Form" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/40/Ryu_Ryu_no_Mi%2C_Model_Brachiosaurus_Beast_Form.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221106024038" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ryu Ryu no Mi, Model Brachiosaurus Beast Form.png" data-image-key="Ryu_Ryu_no_Mi%2C_Model_Brachiosaurus_Beast_Form.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/40/Ryu_Ryu_no_Mi%2C_Model_Brachiosaurus_Beast_Form.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221106024038" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ryu_Ryu_no_Mi,_Model_Brachiosaurus_Beast_Form.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Queen in his full brachiosaurus form.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Queen ate the Ryu Ryu no Mi, Model: Brachiosaurus, an <a href="/wiki/Zoan#Ancient_Zoan" title="Zoan">Ancient Zoan</a>-type <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> that allows him to transform into a full brachiosaurus and a human-brachiosaurus hybrid at will. When fully transformed, Queen becomes much bigger and towers over even large humans like <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a>, who stands over 8 meters tall.<sup id="cite_ref-c945_23-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c945-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As a Zoan, he gains a significant boost to his physical abilities, and as an Ancient Zoan, this attribute is magnified several times over due to the immense toughness of his dinosaur hide. He has tremendous durability in this state, as he has been able to shrug off powerful attacks, including: <a href="/wiki/Black_Leg_Style/Diable_Jambe" title="Black Leg Style/Diable Jambe">Diable Jambe</a>-enhanced kicks from Sanji, strikes from Chopper in <a href="/wiki/Hito_Hito_no_Mi#Monster_Point" title="Hito Hito no Mi">Monster Point</a>, <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Perospero" title="Charlotte Perospero">Perospero</a>'s candy arrows, his own rocket launchers misfiring on him twice, and he was even able to quickly recover after taking two hits from the Former <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Emperor</a> Big Mom, one of the most powerful combatants in the world.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He can use the signature long neck of a brachiosaurus in combat, such as by swinging his head at his opponents, or using his long neck to reach targets that are further than he can normally reach or in mid-air, a skill that can be enhanced due to his extendable, cybernetic neck.<sup id="cite_ref-c989_61-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c989-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> Additionally, his body weight is drastically increased in his dinosaur form, and he can use this immense weight to his advantage, as very little will be able to withstand the crushing pressure of his massive, transformed body. In his Human-Beast Form, Queen generally favours the usage of his cybernetic enchantments and swordsmanship, but fully employs the power and weight of his extremely dense dinosaur body in his Beast Form. 
</p><p>In Beast Form, Queen also possesses the abnormal ability to detach his neck and tail from his torso, effectively allowing him to transform into a large snake with a powerful coil that he claims can even crush the bones and innards of Armament Haki masters.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Haki">Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D32&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>Queen is able to utilize both basic Haki-types. However, he rarely uses either in combat, being more reliant on his Devil Fruit ability and cyborg modifications.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Armament_Haki">Armament Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D33&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7e/Queen_Using_Armament_Haki.png/revision/latest?cb=20220623070317" class="image"><img alt="Queen Using Armament Haki" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="138" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Queen Using Armament Haki.png" data-image-key="Queen_Using_Armament_Haki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7e/Queen_Using_Armament_Haki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20220623070317" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7e/Queen_Using_Armament_Haki.png/revision/latest?cb=20220623070317" class="image"><img alt="Queen Using Armament Haki" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7e/Queen_Using_Armament_Haki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20220623070317" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="138" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Queen Using Armament Haki.png" data-image-key="Queen_Using_Armament_Haki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7e/Queen_Using_Armament_Haki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20220623070317" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Queen_Using_Armament_Haki.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Queen uses Armament Haki to defend himself against Sanji.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Queen is capable of using <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament Haki</a> to harden his arm in order to defend against attacks.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Observation_Haki">Observation Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D34&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Queen possesses the ability to use <a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki" title="Haki/Observation Haki">Observation Haki</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_6-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Weapons">Weapons</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D35&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Queen carries two dao sword on his hips, which are proportionate to his body but rival the size of normal people. He was first shown using one of them to hurt <a href="/wiki/X_Drake" title="X Drake">X Drake</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> In the anime he even demonstrated enough skill wielding both swords to completely nullifyy Marco's <a href="/wiki/Tori_Tori_no_Mi,_Model:_Phoenix" title="Tori Tori no Mi, Model: Phoenix"><i>Bluebird</i></a> attack as well.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> However, one of them was shattered by Sanji when Queen attempted to strike him.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/eb/Queen%27s_Gatling_Gun.png/revision/latest?cb=20211205051648" class="image"><img alt="Queen&#39;s Gatling Gun" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="119" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Queen&#39;s Gatling Gun.png" data-image-key="Queen%27s_Gatling_Gun.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/eb/Queen%27s_Gatling_Gun.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20211205051648" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/eb/Queen%27s_Gatling_Gun.png/revision/latest?cb=20211205051648" class="image"><img alt="Queen&#39;s Gatling Gun" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/eb/Queen%27s_Gatling_Gun.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20211205051648" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="119" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Queen&#39;s Gatling Gun.png" data-image-key="Queen%27s_Gatling_Gun.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/eb/Queen%27s_Gatling_Gun.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20211205051648" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Queen%27s_Gatling_Gun.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Queen's Gatling gun.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>At Onigashima, Queen used a Gatling gun to attack the rebels of the <a href="/wiki/Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai_Alliance" title="Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance">Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c991_67-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c991-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> The gun is loaded with Excite Bullets carrying Ice Oni, Queen's masterpiece virus according to himself.<sup id="cite_ref-c993_59-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c993-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> The gun was eventually destroyed by Zoro.<sup id="cite_ref-c997p11_33-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c997p11-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> Queen also carried a large pistol, but Marco kicked him into a tower before he could use it.<sup id="cite_ref-c1006p17-18_44-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1006p17-18-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Twenty years ago, during the battle against Oden and the Nine Red Scabbards, Queen used a torch as a club.<sup id="cite_ref-c970_43-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c970-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> While a part of <a href="/wiki/MADS" title="MADS">MADS</a>, Queen wielded a large broadsword.<sup id="cite_ref-c1070_68-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1070-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D36&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Past">Past</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D37&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Scien was born 56 years ago on the <a href="/wiki/Grand_Line" title="Grand Line">Grand Line</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_6-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> As a child he appeared to already have a knack for science as he conducted a minilab experiment.<sup id="cite_ref-sbs103_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs103-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9a/MADS_Members.png/revision/latest?cb=20230919224736" class="image"><img alt="MADS Members" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="224" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="MADS Members.png" data-image-key="MADS_Members.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9a/MADS_Members.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230919224736" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9a/MADS_Members.png/revision/latest?cb=20230919224736" class="image"><img alt="MADS Members" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9a/MADS_Members.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230919224736" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="224" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="MADS Members.png" data-image-key="MADS_Members.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9a/MADS_Members.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230919224736" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:MADS_Members.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Scien as part of MADS.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>At some point, he became a scientist and, 39 years ago,<sup id="cite_ref-vc2_7-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vc2-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> joined <a href="/wiki/MADS" title="MADS">MADS</a>, an illegal research team.<sup id="cite_ref-c1070_68-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1070-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>36 years ago, Scien had a child with an unknown woman. 33 years ago, <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a> offered Scien a place in his crew, but Scien chose to continue in MADS.<sup id="cite_ref-vc2_7-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vc2-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> During his stay with MADS, Scien dedicated himself to designing dangerous viruses and he was upset when <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk" title="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</a> won the Ibel Peace Prize. He later mechanized his left arm and frequently competed with <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar Clown</a> and <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Judge" title="Vinsmoke Judge">Vinsmoke Judge</a> to be recognized as the group's second-best scientist.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> Some time later, the group discovered the <a href="/wiki/Lineage_Factor" title="Lineage Factor">Lineage Factor</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> which they used to successfully create a <a href="/wiki/Stussy" title="Stussy">clone</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>29 years ago, Scien decided to leave MADS,<sup id="cite_ref-vc2_7-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vc2-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> which the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a> three years later deemed a threat and forcibly disbanded, arresting some of the scientists.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> Not long after MADS was disbanded, Scien abandoned his 10-year-old child<sup id="cite_ref-vc2_7-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vc2-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> and joined the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a>, settling in <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a> and going under the name "Queen". 23 years ago, Queen participated in the crew's battle against the <a href="/wiki/Gecko_Pirates" title="Gecko Pirates">Gecko Pirates</a> in <a href="/wiki/Ringo" title="Ringo">Ringo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Twenty years ago, when <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Nine_Red_Scabbards" title="Nine Red Scabbards">Nine Red Scabbards</a> were on their way to <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a>, the Beasts Pirates confronted them in the Udon region. In the ensuing battle, Queen fought <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Kanjuro" title="Kurozumi Kanjuro">Kanjuro</a> and <a href="/wiki/Denjiro" title="Denjiro">Denjiro</a>. In the end, Oden and his allies were overwhelmed.<sup id="cite_ref-c970_43-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c970-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Queen, along with <a href="/wiki/King" title="King">King</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a>, was present when <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a> set <a href="/wiki/Kuri#Kuri_Castle" title="Kuri">Oden Castle</a> ablaze in order to kill the <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Family" title="Kouzuki Family">Kouzuki Family</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>4 years ago, Queen left Onigashima along with Kaidou and other main crew members on an expedition.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Saga">Wano Country Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D38&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Arc">Wano Country Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D39&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Queen was on <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a> with King as the two of them reprimanded Jack for collecting an insufficient tribute from <a href="/wiki/Kuri" title="Kuri">his region</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c925_2-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c925-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Some time later, Queen arrived at <a href="/wiki/Prisoner_Mine" title="Prisoner Mine">Prisoner Mine</a> along with some subordinates.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> After looking at a photo of the oiran <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Hiyori" title="Kouzuki Hiyori">Komurasaki</a> and deciding to go to the Pleasure Hall, he gave a musical performance to his subordinates. However, Queen was shocked when <a href="/wiki/Babanuki" title="Babanuki">Babanuki</a> informed him about <a href="/wiki/Eustass_Kid" title="Eustass Kid">Eustass Kid</a>'s escape, the theft of the handcuff keys, and that <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> was trying to escape right there. Once the latter was captured, along with the old yakuza leader <a href="/wiki/Hyougoro" title="Hyougoro">Hyougoro</a>, the All-Star proposed to the young pirate to join the Beast Pirates and be forgiven, but he was rejected. Where then he became nostalgic when he saw Hyougoro and was amused that a legend like this had such a regrettable death. Although Hyougoro wanted him to spare only Luffy, Queen didn't care and decided to have fun with the two prisoners.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Therefore, he ordered to prepare his "Sumo Inferno" and put explosive collars on both Luffy and Hyougoro. He then explained to the duo that they were going to fight the Beast Pirates together in a ring until they were expelled, which would cause the necklaces to explode. While Queen explained to Luffy that he still had the option of joining them and simply being forgiven, he pointed out that the Beast Pirates would have the advantage during duels. However, he decided to free the two prisoners from their Seastone cuffs, although he then reminded Luffy, who was grateful, that they would continue using the explosive collars. Although Hyougoro begged to fight just so as not to get in the way, Luffy threatened and insulted Queen, telling him that he would escape from there by defeating him. The All-Star then sent a group of his subordinates to fight in the ring, however, they were quickly knocked out by Luffy's <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a>, leaving Queen impressed.<sup id="cite_ref-c936_16-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c936-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As he continued to watch Luffy defeat the opponents in the ring, Queen overheard <a href="/wiki/Daifugo" title="Daifugo">Daifugo</a> comment that the execution would have ended sooner if he had been fighting in the ring; to which she replied that it wouldn't have been fun, and then ordered another plate of oshiruko.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later, when <a href="/wiki/Alpacaman" title="Alpacaman">Alpacaman</a> and <a href="/wiki/Madilloman" title="Madilloman">Madilloman</a> were next to fight, Queen mocked his subordinates when they believed that the Gifters would win easily, where she would then watch as Alpacaman would be defeated by Hyougoro.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> Once Madilloman was also defeated along with other fighters Gifters, Queen began to feel somewhat dissatisfied. Finally when night came, he suspended the event until the next morning.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The next day, Kaidou informed him that Komurasaki had died, leaving him devastated. Then he himself went up to the ring where he was surprised to see Hyougoro and Luffy very fat. However, he decided to ignore it and verify Komurasaki's death, so he turned on a <a href="/wiki/Animal_Species/Wano_Country_Saga#Picture_Tanishi" title="Animal Species/Wano Country Saga">Picture Tanishi</a> to project live images from the <a href="/wiki/Flower_Capital" title="Flower Capital">Flower Capital</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c941_28-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c941-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> After witnessing <a href="/wiki/Shimotsuki_Yasuie" title="Shimotsuki Yasuie">Shimotsuki Yasuie</a>'s execution, Queen expressed her approval of Orochi's cruelty.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> He later saw Luffy's companions causing chaos at the execution site, where he was amused to see that they wanted to assassinate the shogun. 
</p><p>Immediately afterwards, Babanuki informed Queen that they had brought <a href="/wiki/Killer" title="Killer">Kamazo</a> and the recaptured Eustass Kid. Then, to add a new element to the game, Queen began to torture the latter two by putting them face down in a tub of water and submerging them, declaring that he would only release them if Hyougoro and Luffy died. When the latter assured him that Kid and Kamazo had nothing to do with it, Queen only made fun of how unstable he was becoming. In addition, the All-Star also pointed out that he did not care about the reward that Luffy had, since all humans drown in water. This angered the young pirate, who tried to attack him, but he easily deflected the blow. The All-Star then stated that no one had a chance to defeat them and escape, and that in the end they would all die. When Luffy declared otherwise, Queen heard a loud noise outside the prison, being informed by his subordinates that communication with the guards outside was cut off.<sup id="cite_ref-c944_17-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c944-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/53/Big_Mom_Attacks_Queen.png/revision/latest?cb=20230314034947" class="image"><img alt="Big Mom Attacks Queen" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Big Mom Attacks Queen.png" data-image-key="Big_Mom_Attacks_Queen.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/53/Big_Mom_Attacks_Queen.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230314034947" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/53/Big_Mom_Attacks_Queen.png/revision/latest?cb=20230314034947" class="image"><img alt="Big Mom Attacks Queen" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/53/Big_Mom_Attacks_Queen.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230314034947" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Big Mom Attacks Queen.png" data-image-key="Big_Mom_Attacks_Queen.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/53/Big_Mom_Attacks_Queen.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230314034947" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Big_Mom_Attacks_Queen.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Big Mom attacks Queen after he refuses to share his oshiruko.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Suddenly, he was shocked when the amnesiac Big Mom appeared breaking through the prison doors, having heard that her ship was sunk by King. When Big Mom ordered oshiroku, Queen told her not to share it and transformed into his <a href="/wiki/Ryu_Ryu_no_Mi,_Model:_Brachiosaurus" title="Ryu Ryu no Mi, Model: Brachiosaurus">brachiosaurus</a> form. However, Big Mom jumped into the air and slammed Queen's head into the ground,<sup id="cite_ref-c945_23-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c945-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> spinning him around and throwing him into a wall. Despite that, he still maintained consciousness, as he listened to how Luffy had eaten the entire oshiruko.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> When Queen finally recovered, he formed a strategy with his subordinates to stop Big Mom, where he would wait at the top of a cliff for her to return to the same point. Once this happened, Queen took advantage of the fact that Big Mom was distracted with the oshiruko pot as a decoy and transformed again to hit her with a headbutt. However, this only caused Big Mom to regain her memory, so Queen believed it was the end, but the Emperor fell asleep at that moment. The All-Star then immediately ordered her to be chained with Seastone and sedated with 100 injections of beast tranquilizers as he prepared a convoy to take her to Onigashima as quickly as possible. Queen set sail with this convoy, leaving the Prisoner Mine in the hands of Babanuki and a small portion of the guards.<sup id="cite_ref-c947_19-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c947-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Upon arriving at Onigashima, Queen rejoined the other All-Stars, where he scolded King for not eliminating Big Mom and angrily told Jack that he had brought her there because of the communications cut in Udon. After King refused to join Big Mom, the Emperor asked for her handcuffs to be removed, so Queen angrily rejected this. However, Kaidou arrived and ordered them to release her, and then watched the clash between the two Emperors in fear.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> The next day, as battle threatened the entire island, Queen tried to find an excuse to return to Udon. However, Babanuki called him to inform him that everything was in order at the Prisoner Mine.<sup id="cite_ref-c952_20-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c952-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later, when Kaidou and Big Mom stopped fighting, King informed Queen about the return of the <a href="/wiki/Numbers" title="Numbers">Numbers</a> for the final banquet of the <a href="/wiki/Fire_Festival" title="Fire Festival">Fire Festival</a>, which displeased him. At that moment, the two Emperors declared to form an alliance with the purpose of taking over the world, leaving Queen surprised.<sup id="cite_ref-c954_27-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c954-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At some point before the festival began, Queen learned that Tobiroppo <a href="/wiki/X_Drake" title="X Drake">X Drake</a> had freed <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Trafalgar Law</a> and therefore wanted to kill him for his betrayal. Therefore, he conspired with <a href="/wiki/Who%27s-Who" title="Who&#39;s-Who">Who's-Who</a> to ambush the traitor.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The day of the Fire Festival arrived, Queen tried to acquire the services of <a href="/wiki/Some" title="Some">Some</a>, a geisha who continually rejected him and whom he now considered his new number one after Komurasaki's death, but she rejected him again saying she had a headache.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 213px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f8/Golden_Kagura.png/revision/latest?cb=20211228154256" class="image"><img alt="Golden Kagura" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="213" height="243" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Golden Kagura.png" data-image-key="Golden_Kagura.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f8/Golden_Kagura.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/213?cb=20211228154256" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f8/Golden_Kagura.png/revision/latest?cb=20211228154256" class="image"><img alt="Golden Kagura" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f8/Golden_Kagura.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/213?cb=20211228154256" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="213" height="243" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Golden Kagura.png" data-image-key="Golden_Kagura.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f8/Golden_Kagura.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/213?cb=20211228154256" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Golden_Kagura.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Queen provides entertainment at the Golden Kagura in Onigashima.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later he enjoyed the celebration, where he demanded large quantities of oshiruko from his subordinates, but they told him that they would take it to Big Mom, to which he yelled at them to prepare more.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup> Then, he headed to the Live Stage to begin the Beasts Pirates' Golden Kagura festivities, where he performed a musical performance for all who would participate.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup> However, soon afterward an uproar broke out on the Live Floor, where Apoo informed him that Luffy, who had in fact escaped from the Prison Mine, as well as his crewmate Roronoa Zoro began. While Apoo asked her the plan to catch them, Queen understood that what Babanuki had told her was not true; where he then announced that he was going to eliminate one of the Tobiroppo and whoever captured the intruders would get said position. As the two intruders made their way, Apoo attacked them with his powers, where Queen taunted Luffy by watching him faint momentarily from a single attack, however, Apoo was then crushed by Eustass Kid.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> Seeing that the latter had also appeared, Queen once again wondered what had happened in Udon. Then, his subordinates asked for permission to kill the intruders, so Queen granted it.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>Later, he along with the other All-Stars accompanied Kaidou to the live stage when Kouzuki Momonosuke was to be executed by Orochi, where the Emperor declared to the latter his intention to encourage the execution with the announcement of the <a href="/wiki/New_Onigashima_Project" title="New Onigashima Project">New Onigashima Project</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> While Kaidou explained the objectives of the plan, Orochi protested when it was mentioned that weapons factories would also be increased and the inhabitants of Florida's capital would be put to work to turn it into a pirate paradise, so Kaidou decapitated him. The latter then offered Orochi's subordinates to join them or die,<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup> where they accepted. As Kaidou was about to execute Momonosuke, the <a href="/wiki/Nine_Red_Scabbards" title="Nine Red Scabbards">Red Scabbards</a> interrupted the stage, and Queen was amazed and would later see how the samurai pushed Kaido.<sup id="cite_ref-c986_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c986-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When the latter fell to the lower floor, he saw how the <a href="/wiki/Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai_Alliance" title="Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance">Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance</a>'s attack was unleashed, where he then heard Luffy declare that he was going to defeat them all in an all-out war. After mocking this, Queen was surprised when one of his subordinates informed him that thousands of people were entering through the back entrance: the prisoners of <a href="/wiki/Flower_Capital" title="Flower Capital">Rasetsu Town</a> and Udon, Trafagal Law, and even <a href="/wiki/Marco" title="Marco">Marco</a> and <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Perospero" title="Charlotte Perospero">Charlotte Perospero</a>. Then the All-Star announced to everyone to take their weapons and proclaimed that the party is over.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 191px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d1/Queen_Chomps_on_Luffy_and_Zoro.png/revision/latest?cb=20211121170026" class="image"><img alt="Queen Chomps on Luffy and Zoro" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="191" height="137" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Queen Chomps on Luffy and Zoro.png" data-image-key="Queen_Chomps_on_Luffy_and_Zoro.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d1/Queen_Chomps_on_Luffy_and_Zoro.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/191?cb=20211121170026" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d1/Queen_Chomps_on_Luffy_and_Zoro.png/revision/latest?cb=20211121170026" class="image"><img alt="Queen Chomps on Luffy and Zoro" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d1/Queen_Chomps_on_Luffy_and_Zoro.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/191?cb=20211121170026" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="191" height="137" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Queen Chomps on Luffy and Zoro.png" data-image-key="Queen_Chomps_on_Luffy_and_Zoro.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d1/Queen_Chomps_on_Luffy_and_Zoro.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/191?cb=20211121170026" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Queen_Chomps_on_Luffy_and_Zoro.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Queen stops Luffy and Zoro.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After, when Jack went to the roof to support Kaidou against the Red Scabbards, Queen argued with King about this. Suddenly, <a href="/wiki/Shinobu" title="Shinobu">Shinobu</a> appeared to try to free Momonosuke, but King prevented it by throwing her. However, Momonosuke's chains broke, where Queen watched in confusion as the boy floated away. At that moment, King attacked Sanji, who had done so thanks to him being invisible. After the latter managed to get Momonosuke to safety with Shinobu, King proceeded to confront the enemy by throwing him against a building.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup> Shortly after, Luffy arrived at the Live Stage accompanied by Zoro to reach the roof and confront Kaido. Despite telling them to stop, Queen was completely ignored, where he then transformed and stopped them with his mouth before they could cross the hole that led to the rooftop. When King came flying in with a group of flying Gifters to block the way, Queen violently threw Luffy and Zoro to the floor below. However, he later realized that these two were reunited along with the rest of the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hats</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c989_61-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c989-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> After returning to her human form, Queen discussed the situation with King and told him that he did not understand how the Udon prisoners had managed to escape, only to become irritated when his fellow All-Star criticized him for this error. As he puzzledly wondered if what Babanuki told her was because the prisoners forced him, Queen heard King contact the Tobiroppo to prevent the alliance from reaching the roof.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 206px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cd/Queen_and_Who%27s-Who_Ambush_Drake.png/revision/latest?cb=20230317024617" class="image"><img alt="Queen and Who&#39;s-Who Ambush Drake" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="206" height="116" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Queen and Who&#39;s-Who Ambush Drake.png" data-image-key="Queen_and_Who%27s-Who_Ambush_Drake.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cd/Queen_and_Who%27s-Who_Ambush_Drake.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/206?cb=20230317024617" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cd/Queen_and_Who%27s-Who_Ambush_Drake.png/revision/latest?cb=20230317024617" class="image"><img alt="Queen and Who&#39;s-Who Ambush Drake" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cd/Queen_and_Who%27s-Who_Ambush_Drake.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/206?cb=20230317024617" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="206" height="116" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Queen and Who&#39;s-Who Ambush Drake.png" data-image-key="Queen_and_Who%27s-Who_Ambush_Drake.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cd/Queen_and_Who%27s-Who_Ambush_Drake.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/206?cb=20230317024617" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Queen_and_Who%27s-Who_Ambush_Drake.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Queen and Who's-Who ambush Drake.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>He later went to a room in the castle, where <a href="/wiki/Who%27s-Who" title="Who&#39;s-Who">Who's-Who</a> arrived shortly after along with X Drake, and the two attacked the latter. When Drake asked the reason for this, Queen accused him and interrogated him with Who's Who and <a href="/wiki/Basil_Hawkins" title="Basil Hawkins">Basil Hawkins</a> about freeing Law, as well as declaring to Drake that the person he wanted to kill was him. At that moment, the All-Star began to question the traitor about his true loyalty and mission, however, Drake told him not to reveal anything, so Queen mocked him and stated that everyone gives up when they suffer his tortures. But suddenly an explosion occurred that allowed Drake to escape.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After arriving at the Live Floor, he broke up the enemy fight by using a Gatling gun to fire bullets containing his <a href="/wiki/Ice_Oni" title="Ice Oni">Ice Oni</a> virus, and also told Drake not to let him escape. As the virus infection spread among comrades and enemies alike, turning them into frenzied zombies, Queen ordered all exits on that floor closed.<sup id="cite_ref-c991_67-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c991-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> When some Pleasures asked his why he infected them too, he replied that they just laugh and can be more useful that way. Immediately afterwards, Queen announced that the infected would die within the hour and threw the only virus antibody sample to Apoo. Then, the All-Star announced his new massacre game: all the infected can chase Apoo to claim the antidote and the latter will live if he manages to escape, while the others will die.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When he saw Drake attack Apoo, Queen cursed him for joining the alliance side. While he was looking at the posters of the Straw Hats, thought it was better to kill Zoro and Sanji, since these two were the strongest of the crew after the captain; also commenting that one of Vinsmoke Judge's sons is among said crew.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Afterwards, Queen continued to watch the chase of his game, where he taunted Apoo by seeing him run, but Zoro finally knocked out the latter and gave the antibodies to his crewmate <a href="/wiki/Tony_Tony_Chopper" title="Tony Tony Chopper">Tony Tony Chopper</a>, who explained to the infected that they must use fire to stop the advance of the virus, and that he would develop enough antibodies for all of them. Upon hearing this, Queen became angry and prepared to kill Chopper and Apoo with his Gatling gun, but the gun was then destroyed by a flying sword slash from Zoro. He then heard the latter declare that he had not come to the island to waste time in his game, but to finish off Kaidou. Suddenly a strong earthquake was felt throughout the island, where <a href="/wiki/Marco" title="Marco">Marco</a> then arrived flying,<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup> who used his <a href="/wiki/Tori_Tori_no_Mi,_Model:_Phoenix" title="Tori Tori no Mi, Model: Phoenix">flames</a> to temporarily reverse the effects of the Ice Oni. Seeing this, Queen wondered why Marco was there and then ordered some subordinates to retrieve the antidote.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 228px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/54/Marco_Vs._All_Stars.png/revision/latest?cb=20220417055557" class="image"><img alt="Marco Vs" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="228" height="128" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Marco Vs. All Stars.png" data-image-key="Marco_Vs._All_Stars.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/54/Marco_Vs._All_Stars.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/228?cb=20220417055557" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/54/Marco_Vs._All_Stars.png/revision/latest?cb=20220417055557" class="image"><img alt="Marco Vs" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/54/Marco_Vs._All_Stars.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/228?cb=20220417055557" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="228" height="128" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Marco Vs. All Stars.png" data-image-key="Marco_Vs._All_Stars.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/54/Marco_Vs._All_Stars.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/228?cb=20220417055557" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Marco_Vs._All_Stars.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Marco vs. Queen and King.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Shortly after, Queen ordered his subordinates to stop Marco, however, the latter defeated them all and then transformed into his phoenix form to take Zoro to the roof. Once King arrived to support him, both All-Stars transformed into their dinosaur forms and Queen declared to Marco that he would not let him escape easily and that all the samurai would have died by now. After Marco responded that they were stupid for underestimating the New Generation they were facing, Queen shot him with his mouth cannons, but the attack did no damage,<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup> making him wonder if that ability made Marco invincible. The latter immediately restrained both All-Stars with his phoenix wings before throwing Zoro into the ceiling.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He later saw how Hyougoro, who was infected with the Ice Oni virus, was defeating many enemies, so Queen tried to shoot him with a laser beam to prevent the old man from becoming a worse threat; but Marco stopped him by attacking him with such force that he made him cough up blood. When Queen complained to the latter about it, Marco simply reminded him that he was his opponent and that if he wants to hurt any samurai, he must defeat him first. Therefore, the All-Star fired a laser beam at him, only for Marco to dodge it and then proceed to confront King, who would be thrown into a building. After returning to his human form, Queen approached the ruins of the building, only to also be thrown against a building by Marco.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He then heard some of his subordinates ask him why they too had to die for the Ice Oni. However, Queen transformed and then attacked them, calling them cowards and saying that this virus was his masterpiece, and, in a sense, he made it for them. Because of that, he started telling the Pleasures that they missed their chance to get powers and now they're only good for laughs. While to the Waiters, he told them that no matter how much they wait there are no <a href="/wiki/SMILE" title="SMILE">SMILES</a> to give them powers, therefore they can only be useful if they become Ice Oni and eventually die. He also added that he could always replace them and that he has even given some a chance to live by giving them the antidote. When the samurai felt sorry for his subordinates, Queen reprimanded them saying that Chopper was a pirate, therefore the latter would not help them, and surely abandoned them all by using the antidote on himself.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/df/Chopper_Hits_Queen.png/revision/latest?cb=20240720170828" class="image"><img alt="Chopper Hits Queen" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Chopper Hits Queen.png" data-image-key="Chopper_Hits_Queen.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/df/Chopper_Hits_Queen.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240720170828" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/df/Chopper_Hits_Queen.png/revision/latest?cb=20240720170828" class="image"><img alt="Chopper Hits Queen" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/df/Chopper_Hits_Queen.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240720170828" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Chopper Hits Queen.png" data-image-key="Chopper_Hits_Queen.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/df/Chopper_Hits_Queen.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240720170828" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Chopper_Hits_Queen.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Queen being slapped by Chopper.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>However, Chopper appeared shortly after and revealed his <a href="/wiki/Chopperphage" title="Chopperphage">countervirus</a>, which spread through the air and cured all those infected. After the doctor explained how he created the antidote, Queen was left confused as to how the latter had gained all that medical experience to do it. Even though the reindeer told him his answer to this, the All-Star simply ignored him and became even angrier when he noticed that he also cured his subordinates. At that moment, he heard Chopper declare that viruses were not intended to be used as weapons, as even the user would lose control. However, Queen refused to be lectured and tried to kill him with lightning, but just then, the Placers got in the way. Despite ordering them to get out of the way, the Placers replied that they would no longer work for him and that they were now going to protect the one who saved them. At that moment, Marco grabbed Queen by the neck, who would then be beaten by Chopper in his <a href="/wiki/Hito_Hito_no_Mi" title="Hito Hito no Mi">Monster Point</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> The All-Star proceeded to confront the latter, where despite being physically dominated by Chopper at first, Queen noticed how the reindeer was running out of energy. After Chopper dodged one of his lasers, Queen listened to <a href="/wiki/Bao_Huang" title="Bao Huang">Bao Huang</a> announced to the entire island that Luffy had been defeated by Kaidou.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup> As Chopper became sad at this news, Queen proceeded to overpower him, where he then declared to the reindeer that he was just playing with him. But before he could deliver the final blow, Sanji appeared and hit him in the head with a flaming kick, causing his neck to begin to spin. This caused Queen to unknowingly intercept a barrage of <a href="/wiki/Pero_Pero_no_Mi" title="Pero Pero no Mi">candy arrows</a> from Perospero, who would then be expelled from there. Once he regained his balance, the All-Star was upset to see that Judge's son was responsible, so he prepared to confront him. Suddenly, he heard Momonosuke broadcast the announcement that Luffy was still alive and that he would return to defeat Kaidou.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/23/Sanji_vs_Queen.png/revision/latest?cb=20221106030536" class="image"><img alt="Sanji vs Queen" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sanji vs Queen.png" data-image-key="Sanji_vs_Queen.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/23/Sanji_vs_Queen.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20221106030536" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/23/Sanji_vs_Queen.png/revision/latest?cb=20221106030536" class="image"><img alt="Sanji vs Queen" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/23/Sanji_vs_Queen.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20221106030536" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sanji vs Queen.png" data-image-key="Sanji_vs_Queen.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/23/Sanji_vs_Queen.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20221106030536" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sanji_vs_Queen.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Queen vs. Sanji.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Shortly after, King overheard how <a href="/wiki/Bao_Huang" title="Bao Huang">Bao Huang</a> accidentally announced the defeats of <a href="/wiki/Ulti" title="Ulti">Ulti</a> and <a href="/wiki/Page_One" title="Page One">Page One</a>. When, at that moment, <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Tama" title="Kurozumi Tama">Tama</a> appeared on the Live Stage,<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup> Queen yelled at the little girl about what she was doing there and who she was, as well as asking Bao Huang what was going on. After this, Tama ordered those who ate her <a href="/wiki/Kibi_Kibi_no_Mi" title="Kibi Kibi no Mi">kibi dango</a> to help Luffy and Momonosuke defeat Kaido. Even though Queen ordered the girl to be killed, the Gifters began to turn against the crew. After realizing that Tama was responsible for it, he was about to shoot her with a laser beam, but at that moment Sanji attacked him, causing the laser to explode in his mouth. Seeing the latter, Queen recognized him and called him the Judge's son again; to which Sanji angrily told him to stop calling him that, also asking him if he was part of the research group his father was in. Queen replied that they were both part of MADS years ago, where he then transformed into his hybrid form and revealed to his enemy that he was now a <a href="/wiki/Cyborgs" title="Cyborgs">cyborg</a>. When the latter told him that he had already realized, the All-Star assured him that he would not be a match for him anyway,<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup> before shooting him with one of his lasers.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 224px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9c/Queen_and_King_Punish_Traitors.png/revision/latest?cb=20221219014625" class="image"><img alt="Queen and King Punish Traitors" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="224" height="126" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Queen and King Punish Traitors.png" data-image-key="Queen_and_King_Punish_Traitors.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9c/Queen_and_King_Punish_Traitors.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/224?cb=20221219014625" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9c/Queen_and_King_Punish_Traitors.png/revision/latest?cb=20221219014625" class="image"><img alt="Queen and King Punish Traitors" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9c/Queen_and_King_Punish_Traitors.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/224?cb=20221219014625" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="224" height="126" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Queen and King Punish Traitors.png" data-image-key="Queen_and_King_Punish_Traitors.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9c/Queen_and_King_Punish_Traitors.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/224?cb=20221219014625" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Queen_and_King_Punish_Traitors.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Queen and King punish traitors.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later, when King finally joined Queen in the fight, the two began eliminating all the Beast Pirates who betrayed them, with Marco temporarily out of action and Sanji overwhelmed by both. However, the latter managed to get up and proceeded to confront Queen again, while King prepared to eliminate Zoro, who was seriously injured and bandaged. But at that moment, Marco managed to recover and block the attack, where Queen was surprised that he was still alive. As they prepared to permanently eliminate the former member of the <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</a>, who admitted to them that he had nothing left to fight with, Queen and King were attacked by Sanji and Zoro respectively.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Although they fell to the ground, both All-Stars got up unharmed and proceeded to get up, where Queen declared to the two Straw Hats that they would need something better to defeat them, and then shot them with his lasers, although the duo managed to dodge it. Taking advantage of the fact that Zoro was blocking King's attack, Queen was about to attack him with his <i>Bridal Grapper</i>, but Sanji blocked it with his <a href="/wiki/Black_Leg_Style/Diable_Jambe" title="Black Leg Style/Diable Jambe"><i>Diable Jambe</i></a>. When he saw this power, Queen remembered the modifications Judge made to his children, so he asked Sanji if it was because of that. Even though the latter declared that he was human, Queen still believed otherwise, as not just anyone could burst into flames unless they were a <a href="/wiki/Lunarians" title="Lunarians">lunarian</a>. When Sanji gave him a response to this, the All-Star proceeded to defend himself against his opponent's kicks with <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament Haki</a>; adding that he would show him the power of a cyborg that not even Vegapunk can create.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later, Queen was surprised when a huge <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Momonosuke" title="Kouzuki Momonosuke">pink dragon</a> appeared crashing onto the Live Floor.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup> Immediately afterwards, one of the Marys issued a report on the situation on the roof: Yamato was there injured, while Kaidou faced the previous pink dragon, with Luffy riding on him.
