Hearing this, Queen was surprised that Yamato was the one who was restraining Kaidou until now.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/08/Brachiotoguros.png/revision/latest?cb=20230226053251" class="image"><img alt="Brachiotoguros" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Brachiotoguros.png" data-image-key="Brachiotoguros.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/08/Brachiotoguros.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230226053251" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/08/Brachiotoguros.png/revision/latest?cb=20230226053251" class="image"><img alt="Brachiotoguros" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/08/Brachiotoguros.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230226053251" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Brachiotoguros.png" data-image-key="Brachiotoguros.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/08/Brachiotoguros.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230226053251" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Brachiotoguros.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Queen breaks Sanji's bones.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When King began indiscriminately attacking everyone around him on the Live Floor, Queen scolded him for touching him as well; although his fellow All-Star simply replied that he wished he had slit her throat, which angered Queen even more.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup> He then continued fighting Sanji, attacking with his <i>Bry Pan</i>, causing the latter to start having problems. At that moment, the All-Star told Sanji to use the power of the <a href="/wiki/Raid_Suit" title="Raid Suit">Raid Suit</a>, as he knew that he had used it to make himself invisible when facing King. When Queen continued to goad him, calling him <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Family" title="Vinsmoke Family">Vinsmoke</a>, Sanji angrily told him not to call him that and refused to use the Raid Suit due to his hatred for the <a href="/wiki/Germa_66" title="Germa 66">Germa 66</a>. Queen then shot him with his <i>Black Coffee</i>, which his opponent managed to dodge, where the latter proceeded to attack him again with <i>Bien Cuit: Grill Shot</i>. After the attack knocked him down a bit, Queen transformed into his brachiosaurus form and praised Sanji for the strength of his kick. He then decided to show the "true power" of his fruit, so he used his <i>Brachiotoguros</i> technique, causing his tail and neck to split from his body to wrap around Sanji like a snake. As he crushed him, Queen mocked his opponent for letting his guard down, where he also pointed out that not even the strongest Armament Haki user has resisted. After saying that he was disappointed, he again asked Sanji to use the power of the Germa 66 and in exchange he would let him go. When the latter still refused, Queen proceeded to explain to him about the missiles installed in his empty torso that are activated with his voice command, but these attacked him when he named them by mistake. Despite being enraged by this, he only managed to name them a second time, getting attacked again and freeing Sanji in the process.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 195px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Queen%27s_Blade_Shatters_Against_Sanji.png/revision/latest?cb=20230508193740" class="image"><img alt="Queen&#39;s Blade Shatters Against Sanji" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="195" height="128" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Queen&#39;s Blade Shatters Against Sanji.png" data-image-key="Queen%27s_Blade_Shatters_Against_Sanji.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Queen%27s_Blade_Shatters_Against_Sanji.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/195?cb=20230508193740" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Queen%27s_Blade_Shatters_Against_Sanji.png/revision/latest?cb=20230508193740" class="image"><img alt="Queen&#39;s Blade Shatters Against Sanji" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Queen%27s_Blade_Shatters_Against_Sanji.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/195?cb=20230508193740" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="195" height="128" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Queen&#39;s Blade Shatters Against Sanji.png" data-image-key="Queen%27s_Blade_Shatters_Against_Sanji.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Queen%27s_Blade_Shatters_Against_Sanji.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/195?cb=20230508193740" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Queen%27s_Blade_Shatters_Against_Sanji.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Queen's sword breaks while trying to kill Sanji.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Although Queen believed that the opponent must have already been very injured by the grip, Sanji managed to recover as if nothing had happened. When the All-Star reassembled the two parts of his body and transformed into his hybrid form, he attempted to decapitate Sanji with one of his swords, although it ended up breaking, much to his surprise.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup> Knowing that it couldn't have been Armament Haki, he recalled how Judge wanted to create <a href="/wiki/Modified_Humans" title="Modified Humans">modified humans</a> with exoskeletons, who had better stamina, physical strength and quick healing, as well as an unfeeling heart. At that moment, Queen began to fire his laser beams at Sanji, who began to flee; while some of his subordinates shot the latter with his bullets, but they didn't work against Sanji. Seeing this, Queen marveled and began to pursue his target, again asking him to use the Raid Suit to demonstrate the science of the Germa.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After a small confrontation,<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup> he ended up chasing Sanji, where Some suddenly appeared in the way.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup> Seeing that the geisha was really healthy, Queen became invisible and beat her for deceiving him.<sup id="cite_ref-c1034_40-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1034-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> Then he arrived at the Pleasure Hall, where he appeared in front of Sanji in his brachiosaurus form and then transformed into his hybrid form to face him again. Suddenly, he watched eagerly as Sanji finally pulled out the Raid Suit; however, the latter simply destroyed it, leaving Queen completely frustrated. After hearing Sanji contact Zoro, the All-Star saw his opponent disappear, so he asked him if it was scientific enhancement, where he was then violently attacked by Sanji, who told him not to make him angry anymore.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup> Although the attack sent him through many rooms, Queen managed to recover and then explained to Sanji that Zoro could not defeat King, as the latter was a survivor of the Lunarians; telling him that this race was capable of surviving in any environment and in the past they were called "gods". When Sanji asked how they became extinct, Queen replied that he would have to find out himself and then shot him with a laser beam.<sup id="cite_ref-c1033_30-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1033-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When he continued to confront Sanji, the All-Star attacked him with his <i>Sparking Queen</i>, although Sanji managed to avoid it. He then used his <i>Henry Queen</i>, electrocuting the opponent with such force that he fell to the ground injured. At that moment, as he continued to shoot him with more lasers from his eyes, Queen revealed to Sanji that he copied the powers of the Germa 66, as Judge's children are the culmination of her scientific work. Furthermore, he explained to his opponent that he was going to show them to him when the latter had put on the Raid Suit, since by defeating him in this way he would prove to be a better scientist than Judge. When Sanji told him not to involve him in it, Queen grabbed his opponent with his robotic arm and confessed that he had played dumb earlier; explaining to Sanji that he had researched all of Germa's science and had therefore copied the abilities of the latter's brothers. Queen then proceeded to use the <i>Winch Queen</i>, spinning Sanji through several walls. However, the adversary was able to escape destroying the All-Star's mechanical arm, who angrily asked him how dare he. Sanji then stood up and reminded him not to talk about the Vinsmoke Family, so Queen scolded him for believing he could control his right to free speech. Without wasting time, Sanji used <i>Flanchet Flyer</i> to attack Queen directly in the stomach, who despite resisting the attack felt great pain. Seeing this, Sanji told the All-Star that he was wrong if he believed that he had the fight dominated, since there was no way that his kick would not have had an effect on him and that they were both exhausted.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 199px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/eb/Queen_defeated.png/revision/latest?cb=20230512195724" class="image"><img alt="Queen defeated" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="199" height="164" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Queen defeated.png" data-image-key="Queen_defeated.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/eb/Queen_defeated.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/199?cb=20230512195724" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/eb/Queen_defeated.png/revision/latest?cb=20230512195724" class="image"><img alt="Queen defeated" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/eb/Queen_defeated.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/199?cb=20230512195724" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="199" height="164" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Queen defeated.png" data-image-key="Queen_defeated.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/eb/Queen_defeated.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/199?cb=20230512195724" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Queen_defeated.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Queen is defeated and sent off Onigashima by Sanji.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After hearing his opponent declare that he had accepted his fate and was not the same person he fought on the Life Floor, Queen proceeded to turn invisible and asked Sanji to prove to him if he was telling the truth about it. The latter then disappeared, surprising Queen as the Raid Suit had been destroyed, but he then realized that Sanji did not turn invisible, but rather he was moving faster than the eye can see. When Queen decided to wait until the enemy ran out of energy to defeat him, he saw Some, who was chasing her <a href="/wiki/Chuji" title="Chuji">pet mouse</a>. Seeing that the geisha had recovered, the All-Star decided to give her another blow as punishment. However, Sanji then hit him with several techniques from his new <a href="/wiki/Black_Leg_Style/Ifrit_Jambe" title="Black Leg Style/Ifrit Jambe"><i>Ifrit Jambe</i></a>, which ended up defeating Queen,<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup> and sending him flying out of Onigashima.<sup id="cite_ref-c1035_36-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1035-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ec/Ryokugyu_Subdues_Queen.png/revision/latest?cb=20231122013452" class="image"><img alt="Ryokugyu Subdues Queen" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="151" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ryokugyu Subdues Queen.png" data-image-key="Ryokugyu_Subdues_Queen.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ec/Ryokugyu_Subdues_Queen.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231122013452" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ec/Ryokugyu_Subdues_Queen.png/revision/latest?cb=20231122013452" class="image"><img alt="Ryokugyu Subdues Queen" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ec/Ryokugyu_Subdues_Queen.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231122013452" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="151" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ryokugyu Subdues Queen.png" data-image-key="Ryokugyu_Subdues_Queen.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ec/Ryokugyu_Subdues_Queen.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231122013452" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ryokugyu_Subdues_Queen.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Queen is subdued by Ryokugyu.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Following the alliance's victory, Queen was located at the former Prisoner Mine along with King and many other crew members. A week later, <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">Admiral</a> <a href="/wiki/Aramaki" title="Aramaki">Ryokugyu</a> came and attacked the complex, impaling Queen with a <a href="/wiki/Mori_Mori_no_Mi" title="Mori Mori no Mi">tree branch</a> which rapidly dehydrated him and made him shrink considerably. Queen demanded to maintain his weight, but Ryokugyu then brutally stomped on Queen multiple times. Ryokugyu then requested a battleship to be sent to Wano, presumably to detain Queen and his crewmates.<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Anime_and_Manga_Differences">Anime and Manga Differences</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D42&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/17/Queen_20_Years_Ago.png/revision/latest?cb=20210627214444" class="image"><img alt="Queen 20 Years Ago" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="210" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Queen 20 Years Ago.png" data-image-key="Queen_20_Years_Ago.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/17/Queen_20_Years_Ago.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210627214444" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/17/Queen_20_Years_Ago.png/revision/latest?cb=20210627214444" class="image"><img alt="Queen 20 Years Ago" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/17/Queen_20_Years_Ago.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210627214444" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="210" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Queen 20 Years Ago.png" data-image-key="Queen_20_Years_Ago.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/17/Queen_20_Years_Ago.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210627214444" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Queen_20_Years_Ago.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Queen incorrectly depicted without a prosthetic arm.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the anime, at the time the <a href="/wiki/Nine_Red_Scabbards" title="Nine Red Scabbards">Nine Red Scabbards</a> were formed while Queen was 36 years old, he appeared to not not have a mechanical left arm. This contradicts his last known appearance while a member of <a href="/wiki/MADS" title="MADS">MADS</a>.
<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Merchandise">Merchandise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D43&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Video_Games">Video Games</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D44&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Playable_Appearances">Playable Appearances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D45&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Treasure_Cruise" title="One Piece Treasure Cruise">One Piece Treasure Cruise</a></i></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Thousand_Storm" title="One Piece Thousand Storm">One Piece Thousand Storm</a></i></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Bounty_Rush" title="One Piece Bounty Rush">One Piece Bounty Rush</a></i></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FQueen%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D46&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Like his fellow <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates#All-Stars" title="Beasts Pirates">All-Stars</a> <a href="/wiki/King" title="King">King</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a>, Queen is named after the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Queen_(playing_card)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Queen (playing card)">playing card rank</a>, fitting with the card-themed names of the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup>
<ul><li>His birth name, "Scien", likely originates from the Japanese pronunciations of the English words "Science"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">サイエンス</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Saiensu</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> or "Scientist"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">サイエンティスト</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Saiensutisuto</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>, in relation to his favorite field and former job at <a href="/wiki/MADS" title="MADS">MADS</a>.</li></ul></li>
<li>Queen's appearance is reminiscent of the character <a href="https://hokuto.fandom.com/wiki/Heart" class="extiw" title="w:c:hokuto:Heart">Heart</a> from <a href="https://hokuto.fandom.com/wiki/Hokuto_no_Ken" class="extiw" title="w:c:hokuto:Hokuto no Ken"><i>Fist of the North Star</i></a>.</li>
<li>He also seems to take some visual cues from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Obelix" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Obelix">Obelix</a>, a character from the Franco-Belgian comic <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Asterix" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Asterix"><i>The Adventures of Asterix</i></a>.
<ul><li>Further evocative of this similarity is their shared affinity for <a href="/wiki/Animal_Species/Wano_Country_Saga#Wild_Boars" title="Animal Species/Wano Country Saga">wild boars</a>, though Queen uses the creatures as a means of transport rather than a food source.</li></ul></li>
<li>Queen's favorite food is <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shiruko" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Shiruko">oshiruko</a>, and his least favorite foods are <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chazuke" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Chazuke">bubuzuke</a> and low-calorie foods.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_6-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Queen's hobbies are dancing and collecting Komurasaki's <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bromide_(Japanese_culture)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bromide (Japanese culture)">bromides</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vc2_7-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vc2-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Queen's animal resemblance is a plesiosaur.<sup id="cite_ref-vc2_7-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vc2-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
